       <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
        openedSsMenu = null;
 openinSsMenu = null;
 openinLink = null;
 openedLink = null;
 function OpenSsMenu(id){
 	openinSsMenu = $('#childrens-'+id);
 	openinSsMenu.addClass('slideOn');
 	openinSsMenu.slideDown(400);
 }
 function CloseSsMenu(id){
 	openinSsMenu = $('#childrens-'+id);
 	openinSsMenu.slideUp(400,function(){
 		openinSsMenu.removeClass('slideOn');
 	});
 }
 $(document).ready(function(){	
 	var sMenu = null;
 	var OsMenu = null;
 	var nIcon = null;
 	var OnIcon = null;
 	var nItem = null;
 	var OnItem = null;
 	var id = null;
 	$(window).scroll(function (handler) {
 		if ($('#navigation').hasClass('fixed')) {
 			if ($(this).scrollTop() > $('#navigation').height()) {
 			
 				if( !$('#navigation').hasClass('bgPerso')){
 					$('#navigation').css({'background-color':'#fff'});
 					//if ( $('#navigation').hasClass('inverse'))$('#navigation').css('background-color','#000');
 				}
 				$('#navigation').css({'box-shadow':'1px 6px 6px 1px rgba(55,55,55,0.6)'});
 			}
 			if ($(this).scrollTop() < $('#navigation').height()) {
 				if(!$('#navigation').hasClass('bgPerso')){
 					$('#navigation').css({'background-color':'transparent'});
 				}
 				$('#navigation').css({'box-shadow':'none'});
 			}
 		}
 		
 	});
 	$('#navigation .navbar-item').each(function(){
 		id = $(this).attr('id').split('-')[1];
 		
 		$(this).bind('click',function(){
 			
 			id = $(this).attr('id').split('-')[1];
 			nIcon = $('.navbar-icon',this);
 			nItem = $(this);
 			sMenu = $('#Children-'+id);
 			if(sMenu.is(":hidden")){
 				if(OsMenu != null){
 					OsMenu.slideUp(400,function(){
 						if(OsMenu != null){OsMenu.removeClass('slideOn');}
 						if(OnItem != null){OnItem.removeClass('slideOn');}
 						if(OnIcon != null){OnIcon.hide();}
 						
 						sMenu.addClass('slideOn');
 						nItem.addClass('slideOn');
 						sMenu.slideDown(400);
 						nIcon.show();
 						OsMenu = sMenu;
 						OnIcon = nIcon;
 						OnItem = nItem;
 					});
 				}else{
 					sMenu.addClass('slideOn');
 					nItem.addClass('slideOn');
 					sMenu.slideDown(400);
 					nIcon.show();
 					OsMenu = sMenu;
 					OnIcon = nIcon;
 				}
 			}else{
 				sMenu.slideUp(400,function(){
 					sMenu.removeClass('slideOn');
 					nItem.removeClass('slideOn');
 					nIcon.hide();
 					OsMenu = null;
 
 				});
 			}
 			$(OsMenu).mouseleave(function(){
 				sMenu.slideUp(400,function(){
 					sMenu.removeClass('slideOn');
 					nIcon.hide();
 					OsMenu = null;
 				});
 			});
 				
 			
 			
 			
 		});
 		
 	});
 	
 	
 	
 	
 	$('.navbar-children .collapse').each(function(){
 		var id=$(this).attr('id').split('-')[1];
 		$('#btn-'+id+' .btn-collapse span').addClass('glyphicon-triangle-right');
 		$(this).on('show.bs.collapse', function () {
 			$('#btn-'+id).addClass('open');
 			$('#btn-'+id+' .btn-collapse span').removeClass('glyphicon-triangle-right');
 			$('#btn-'+id+' .btn-collapse span').addClass('glyphicon-triangle-bottom');
 		});
 		$(this).on('hide.bs.collapse', function () {
 			$('#btn-'+id).removeClass('open');
 			$('#btn-'+id+' .btn-collapse span').removeClass('glyphicon-triangle-bottom');
 			$('#btn-'+id+' .btn-collapse span').addClass('glyphicon-triangle-right');
 		});
 		$(this).on('shown.bs.collapse', function () {
 			$('#btn-'+id).addClass('open');
 			$('#btn-'+id+' .btn-collapse span').removeClass('glyphicon-triangle-right');
 			$('#btn-'+id+' .btn-collapse span').addClass('glyphicon-triangle-bottom');
 		});
 		$(this).on('hidden.bs.collapse', function () {
 			$('#btn-'+id).removeClass('open');
 			$('#btn-'+id+' .btn-collapse span').removeClass('glyphicon-triangle-bottom');
 			$('#btn-'+id+' .btn-collapse span').addClass('glyphicon-triangle-right');
 		});
 	});
 	$('.children-outils').each(function(){
 		var id = $(this).attr('id').split('-')[1];
 		$('.folddown',$(this)).click(function(){
 			$('#Children-'+id+' .collapse').each(function(){
 				$(this).collapse('show');
 			});
 		});
 		$('.foldup',$(this)).click(function(){
 			$('#Children-'+id+' .collapse').each(function(){
 				$(this).collapse('hide');
 			});
 		});
 	});
 	
 	$('#navmobile-closed').click(function(){
 		$('#navmobile').offcanvas('hide');
 	});
 
 });
       </script>

        <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
         $(document).ready(function() {
 		var couleurs = [	"rgba(219,56,92, 0.6)","rgba(104,197,255, 0.6)",
 							"rgba(151,90,193, 0.6)", "rgba(193,70,136, 0.6)",

 							"rgba(255,156,0, 0.6)", "rgba(244,71,164, 0.6)",
 							"rgba(32,187,185, 0.6)", "rgba(76,180,65, 0.6)",
 							"rgba(57,99,214, 0.6)", "rgba(37,139,116, 0.6)",
 							"rgba(120,101,227, 0.6)", "rgba(255,180,0, 0.6)",
 							"rgba(32,169,255, 0.6)"
 		];
 		
 		var height = 200;
 		$('#list-carousel li span').each(function() {
 			$(this).css('background-color', couleurs[Math.floor(Math.random() * couleurs.length)]);
 		});
 		$('#list-carousel,#list-carousel li,#list-carousel li p').css('height',height+'px');
 		
 		$('#list-carousel').moodular({"step":6,"view":1,"timer":5000,"speed":2000,"direction":"left","effects":"fade "});
 		if( $('#header-cartouche').width() < ($('#header').width()/4)){
 			$('#header-cartouche').width(($('#header').width()/4));
 		}
 		
 		var cartouchePos = 'left';
 		var left = 0;
 		var center = ($('#header-cartouche').parent().width()- $('#header-cartouche').width())/2;
 		var right = $('#header-cartouche').parent().width()- $('#header-cartouche').width();
 		
 		$('#header-cartouche').css('margin-left',left+'px');
 		$('#header-cartouche').slideDown('slow');
 		
 		if(cartouchePos == 'right'){
 			$('#list-carousel li span').css('float','left');
 		}
 });
        </script>
